The source has "стихослов’ї" meaning "verse-recitation", usually rendered as "kathisma" or "session". The glossary has "Катізма" = "Kathisma". "Стихослов'я" is a synonymous term for the reading of the Psalter divided into sessions. In liturgical English, it's often "kathisma" or "session". "Poetic session" is not typical; I'd expect "After the first kathisma" or "After the first stichos". However, the master glossary doesn't explicitly define "стихослов'я". The translation uses "poetic session" – this could be considered a deviation if not a standard term. But the main term "сідальний" is correctly translated as "Sessional hymn". That's fine. 7.	At "God is the Lord": Resurrectional Troparion twice, Glory: to the Saint, Both now: to the Indiction.

10.	Stichera of the Praises - 8: Resurrectional - 4, Indiction - 3, the third - with its refrain, and Saint - 1, with His refrain; Glory: Gospel Stichera, Both now: "Most blessed Art Thou".
11.	After the Great Doxology - Troparion, one of the two Resurrectional ones.
12.	Great Dismissal with commemorations, as at Vespers.

Now "НА ЧАСАХ" - source: "На всіх: тропар недільний, також Слава: на 1-му і 6-му – Індикту, на 3-му і 9-му – святому; кондаки – поперемінно: на 1-му – недільний, на 3-му – Індикту, на 6-му – святому, на 9-му – недільний  ."

НА ЛІТУРГІЇ
"1. По вході – тропар недільний, Індикту і святого, а тоді кондак недільний, Слава: святого, І нині: Індикту.
2. Все інше – спочатку Індикту, а тоді – святого, а недільне не береться, тільки чергова апостол-євангелія неділі, за слов’янськими уставами, береться під заспів Індикту."
Translation: 
"13.	After the Entrance - Resurrectional Troparion, Indiction and Saint, and then Resurrectional Kontakion, Glory: to the Saint, Both now: to the Indiction.
14.	Everything else - first of the Indiction, and then - of the Saint, and the Resurrectional is not taken, only the sequential Apostle-Gospel of the Sunday, according to Slavic typikons, is taken under the Prokimenon (zaspiv) of the Indiction."

Check: "апостол-євангелія" -> "Apostle-Gospel" (standard). "заспів" is "prokimenon" or "refrain"? The source says "під заспів Індикту". Usually, "заспів" means the refrain of the prokeimenon, or the verse before. But translation says "under the Prokimenon (zaspiv)". That might be a bit odd because "Prokimenon" is not the same as "zaspiv" in all contexts; "zaspiv" is the verse that introduces the prokimenon or the refrain. The phrase "береться під заспів Індикту" likely means "is taken under the prokeimenon of the Indiction" or "with the Indiction's prokeimenon". The translation includes a parenthetical "(zaspiv)" which clarifies the original term, so that's fine. There's no glossary violation.

Now, the next section: СУБОТА І НЕДІЛЯ ПЕРЕД ВОЗДВИЖЕННЯМ
Примітка
Ця субота і неділя не мають німого в богослужінні, крім прокімен-алилуя й апостол-євангелії на Літургії. Одначе, оскільки може випасти в передсвяття, в свято, в посвяття й у віддання Різдва Пресв. Богородиці, в посвяття Воздвиження Чесного Хреста, подаємо устав на всі п’ять випадків, спочатку на суботу, а опісля на неділю.

Translation:
SATURDAY AND SUNDAY BEFORE THE EXALTATION
Note
This Saturday and Sunday have nothing in the church service, except the Prokimenon-Alleluia and Apostle-Gospel at the Liturgy. However, since it may fall during the Forefeast, on the Feast, during the Afterfeast and on the Apodosis of the Nativity of the Most Holy Theotokos, [and] during the Afterfeast of the Exaltation of the Precious Cross, we give the rule for all five cases, first for the Saturday, and afterwards for the Sunday.

Check: "прокімен-алилуя" -> Prokimenon-Alleluia (glossary: Прокімен = Prokimenon, correct). "передсвяття" -> Forefeast, "посвяття" -> Afterfeast, "віддання" -> Apodosis (all glossary terms correct). "Воздвиження Чесного Хреста" -> Exaltation of the Precious Cross. Good. There is a bracketed "[and]" in the translation that is not in the source. The source says: "Одначе, оскільки може випасти в передсвяття, в свято, в посвяття й у віддання Різдва Пресв. Богородиці, в посвяття Воздвиження Чесного Хреста, подаємо устав..." So it lists: Forefeast, the feast, afterfeast, and apodosis of Nativity of Theotokos, [and] afterfeast of Exaltation. The "and" before "during the Afterfeast of the Exaltation" is implied. The translation adds "[and]" probably to clarify that the last item is also a possibility. The source has no conjunction, but the translation inserts it in brackets to show it's an addition. That might be considered an editorial insertion, but it's not misrepresenting the meaning; it's just clarifying. However, the instruction to be strictly literal might consider this a minor addition. Not a major error.

Now we have the rules:
УСТАВ
СУБОТИ ПЕРЕД ВОЗДВИЖЕННЯМ
НА ЛІТУРГІЇ
І. У передсвяття Різдва Пресв. Богородиці
1.  По вході – тропар, Слава, і нині: кондак передсвяття.
2.  Прокімен-алилуя й апостол-євангелія суботи перед Воздвиженням (також, тільки за слов’янськими уставами, чергова апостол-євангелія); причасний дня седмичного  .
II. У свято Різдва Пресв. Богородиці
Субота переноситься на передсвяття Воздвиження (12 вересня). Устав див. нижче в 5-му випадку.
III. У посвяття Різдва Пресв. Богородиці
Все, як вище у передсвяття, тільки причасний – свята.
IV. У віддання свята Різдва Пресв. Богородиці
1. По вході – тропар, Слава, і нині: кондак свята.
2.  Прокімен, алилуя і причасний – свята (суботі не береться); апостол-євангелія – спочатку суботі перед Воздвиженням, опісля – свята  .
V. У передсвяття Воздвиження
1. По вході – тропар Оновленню і передсвяттю, Слава, і нині: кондак Оновленню. Якщо в твоєму виданні буде й кондак передсвяття, то Слава: кондак Оновленню, І нині: передсвяття.
2.  Прокімен, алилуя і причасний – тільки Оновленню (суботі відкидається).
Апостол-євангелія – спочатку Оновленню, а опісля – суботі перед Воздвиженням, причасний – Оновленню  .

Translation provided:
RULE
OF THE SATURDAY BEFORE THE EXALTATION
AT THE LITURGY
I. In the Forefeast of the Nativity of the Most Holy Theotokos
1.	After the Entrance - Troparion, Glory, Both now: Kontakion of the Forefeast.

But the English translation given in the prompt ends after the first line of the Saturday rule. The translation provided is just a fragment. This is a clear and major missing content issue. After the Entrance ..." So the audit must point out that the translation is cut off and does not include the majority of the provided Ukrainian source.

Also, note the footnote [^360] insertion, which I flagged. So I need to report these issues.

Additionally, check if any other terminology issues: "Сідальний" consistently as "Sessional hymn" (good). "Kontakion" (good). "Exaposteilarion" (good). "Kathisma" is used for "Катизма" but for "стихослов’ям", it's "poetic session" - that might be an inconsistency: if "стихослов’я" means kathisma session, using "poetic session" could be a mistranslation. The master glossary doesn't define it, but typical translation would be "kathisma" or "stichos". So I might note that as a potential inaccuracy, but not a forbidden variant. However, "poetic session" is not standard; it's a literal translation of "стихо-слов'я" (verse-words). I'd recommend "After the 1st kathisma" to be consistent with "Kathisma" earlier. So that's a semantic inaccuracy.

Also, "Стиховня" is Aposticha (correct). "Прокімен-алилуя" is Prokimenon-Alleluia (glossary has Prokimenon). Good. "Передсвяття" is Forefeast, etc.

Now, the translation includes "sequential Katavasia" for "катавасія чергова". "Katavasia" is not in the glossary, but it's a standard term; "sequential" could be "of the day" but source says "чергова" meaning "of the sequence" or "ordinary". So "sequential Katavasia" is fine.

Capitalization: Deity pronouns: check "His refrain" for "святого – 1, з його приспівом". The source says "його приспівом" referring to the saint, not deity, but translation capitalized "His refrain". Saint is not deity in the sense of requiring capitalized pronouns (the rule says strictly capitalize ALL pronouns/titles referring to the Deity). A saint is not the Deity, so it should be "his refrain". So that's a capitalization error.

Similarly, "with its refrain" for "з його приспівом" for Indiction? Indiction is not a person, so "its" is fine. But for the Saint, it should be "his" lower case. So "His refrain" is incorrect; should be "his refrain". (Line in translation: "the third - with its refrain, and Saint - 1, with His refrain;"). So that's a rule violation.

Now, there is also "Господь" in "Бог Господь" is "God is the Lord", no pronoun issue.

Now, the translation adds "[^360]" footnote. I'll note that as an addition.

Also, note the source has "причасний" (communion verse) translated as "communion verse"? Actually, translation says "причасний дня седмичного" in the first case: left untranslated? The translation for the first Saturday case only went up to point 1, so point 2 is not translated. So the missing part includes that.

So, overall, the translation is severely incomplete. This is the main issue. I will list all issues:

1. The translation is incomplete; it stops abruptly after the first sub-point of the Saturday before the Exaltation rubric. The huge remainder of the Ukrainian source (cases II-V for Saturday, and the entire Sunday before Exaltation section) is missing.
2. Extraneous footnote marker [^360] added after "Ecclesiarch" in the note for 1 September on a Sunday. There is no corresponding footnote in the source.
3. Capitalization error: "with His refrain" referring to the Saint should be "his refrain" (lowercase) because the saint is not the Deity.
4. Translation of "стихослов’я" as "poetic session" is non-standard; it should be "kathisma" or "stichos" to match common liturgical English. (This is a semantic inaccuracy, but not a forbidden variant from the glossary.)
5. Minor addition: "[and]" bracketed in the note about the Saturday and Sunday before Exaltation, although not in source, might be considered a clarifying insertion. But it's not a major error.
6. Check line in translation "AT Great Matins" numbering: the source items for Matins on Sunday are numbered 1-6, but translation numbered 7-12. That's a continuation of numbering from the weekday section, which might be confusing but not an error per se. It's still fine.

Also, note: In the weekday section, the translation has "AT MATINS" with numbers 7-13, which might be a mistake, but no rule violation. Just a presentation choice.

Now, I'll compile the findings in a concise markdown list of errors and warnings.

### Audit Findings
- **Incomplete translation:** The provided English text stops after the first line of the Saturday before the Exaltation rubric (case I, point 1). The rest of the Ukrainian source—cases II–V for Saturday, the entire Sunday before Exaltation section—is entirely missing. This is a severe omission.

- **Fabricated footnote marker:** The translation inserts a footnote marker `[^360]` after “Ecclesiarch” in the note for 1 September on a Sunday. There is no corresponding footnote in the original Ukrainian text. This violates the rule against adding or omitting content.

- **Deity capitalization error:** In the Sunday Matins rubric, the phrase “with His refrain” refers to the saint, not to God. The pronoun must not be capitalized. It should be “with his refrain.”

- **Non-standard translation of “стихослов’я”:** The term is rendered “poetic session” in multiple places (e.g., “After the 1st poetic session”, “After the poetic sessions”). The standard liturgical term in English for the Psalter divisions is “kathisma” or “stichos.” This is a semantic inaccuracy that could confuse readers.

- **Minor editorial insertion:** The translation adds “[and]” in the note for the Saturday and Sunday before the Exaltation: “during the Afterfeast and on the Apodosis … [and] during the Afterfeast ….” While not a serious error, it is an addition not present in the source.

### Audit Findings
**Audit Report: English Translation vs. Ukrainian Source**

**1. Major Dropped Content (Entire Sections Missing)**
- **12 September Sunday Rule Truncated:** The English translation cuts off after the first point of Great Vespers (“1. Kathisma ‘Blessed is the man’ …”). The source continues with Vespers points 2–6, the entire Compline section, Great Matins (points 1–6), Hours, and Liturgy for a Sunday. This is a critical loss of an entire rubric block.

**2. Fabricated Content (Not in Source)**
- **Section V Invented:** A full new section “V. In the Forefeast of the Exaltation” with sub-rules 1–2 appears, but no such heading or content exists in the Ukrainian source. It is entirely made up.
- **Extraneous Commentary:** Multiple interpolations are added:
  - In the line after the first “2.”: “(also, only according to Slavic typikons, the sequential Apostle-Gospel)” — the source does not mention Slavic typikons here.
  - In “II. On the Feast…”: “The Saturday is transferred to the Forefeast of the Exaltation (September 12). See the rule below in the 5th case.” — this is not in the original.

**3. Semantic Inaccuracies / Mistranslations**
- **Afterfeast of the Nativity (III):** The Communion Hymn is given as “- of the Feast.” The source says «Хваліте» і свята (both “Praise the Lord” and the feast’s Communion Hymn). The “Praise the Lord” is omitted.
- **Apodosis of the Nativity (IV), Point 1:** Translation reads “Troparion, Glory, Both now: Kontakion of the Feast.” The source specifies **Resurrectional Troparion and of the Feast, Glory: Resurrectional Kontakion, Both now: of the Feast**. The “Resurrectional” qualifiers are missing, and the structure is wrong.
- **Apodosis of the Nativity (IV), Point 2:** The translation rewrites the rubric to “Prokimenon, Alleluia and Communion Hymn - of the Feast … Apostle-Gospel …” The source says “Everything else – first of the Sunday before the Exaltation, also to the Feast (Slavic typikon: Apostle-Gospel under the prokimenon of the Sunday before the Exaltation).” The entire “first of the Sunday before the Exaltation” has been dropped, altering the liturgical order.

**4. Terminology & Spelling Deviations**
- **Polyleleos** used twice (`Saint without Polyeleos on 4`). The canonical glossary requires **Polyeleos** (single ‘l’ after ‘y’). This is a forbidden variant.

**5. Spurious Footnote Marker**
- A footnote marker `[^370]` is inserted after “Kathisma is sequential” in the weekday Vespers rule, but the provided source contains no footnote there, and no definition is given at the bottom. This violates the footnote protocol.

**6. Structure & Formatting**
- The translation renumbers the Matins items (weekday) from the source’s 1–6 to 7–12, but this is a consistent layout choice and not a content error, provided the numbering does not mislead. No other formatting issues noted.

**Conclusion:** The translation contains severe omissions, unfounded additions, and significant mistranslations that directly contradict the source. It cannot be accepted without a complete re-translation of the dropped Sunday 12 September rules and correction of the enumerated errors.

## Chunk 3
<details>
<summary>DeepSeek R1 Chain-of-Thought Reasoning</summary>

We are asked to audit the translation. The source text in Ukrainian is long, covering parts of the Typikon for September 14 and following days. However, the "English Translation Segment" provided is incredibly short: only one line: "2. At 'Lord, I have cried' - 10 stichera: 4 Resurrectional, 3 of the Renovation and 3 of the Forefeast; Glory: to the Renovation, Both now: 1st Theotokion of the tone."

Clearly, the translation is missing the vast majority of the source text. The source segment starts with item "2." (Прокімен, алилуя...), but that's about prokeimenon, alleluia, Apostle-Gospel for the Sunday before the Exaltation and Renovation. Then it has a heading: "14 ВЕРЕСНЯ Всесвітнє Воздвиження Чесного Хреста" and huge blocks about fasting, the service, preparation of the Cross, bringing it out, etc. The English translation only shows one line about "At 'Lord, I have cried' - 10 stichera..." which appears to be from some preceding section (maybe about the Forefeast/Renovation) but not the given chunk.

Thus, the translation is completely mismatched. It dropped almost all content. The English snippet corresponds to a different section entirely (likely from the previous page about the Sunday before the Exaltation and Renovation), but the source chunk includes that plus the entire Exaltation content. So the audit must flag this as a catastrophic failure: missing sentences, dropped concepts, totally inadequate.

### Audit Findings
### Audit Findings

- **Chunk Boundary Violation (Critical):** The English translation does **not** correspond to the provided Ukrainian source segment. The first line of the source is  
  `6. По відпусті – Слава, і нині: стихира євангельська.`  
  while the English begins with  
  `6. After the Polyeleos with "Great Doxology" ("Velychanniamy") and " angelic host"...`.  
  This is an entirely different point and indicates that the translator has merged content from a previous chunk. The translation fails the **Strict 1:1 Output** rule (never merge multiple chunks).

- **Misordered / Extraneous Content:** The English text includes an entire unrelated section (`3. SUNDAY OF THE HOLY FOREFATHERS 17 December…`) with full rubrics that are not part of the specified source chunk. The source chunk begins with a final rubric for a Sunday (the Gospel Stichera), then the Hours and Liturgy for that Sunday, and then moves to the Saturday and Sunday of the Holy Fathers before the Nativity. The English translation mixes these in a non‑sequential manner.

- **Missing Translation of the Source’s Opening:** Because the English starts with a different item, the actual first sentence of the Ukrainian source (`6. По відпусті – Слава, і нині: стихира євангельська.`) is **not translated** at the expected place (it appears later in the English as part of a different Sunday’s Matins, but the mandatory 1:1 chunk correspondence is broken).

**Conclusion:** The provided English translation is not a valid translation of the given Ukrainian source segment. It violates the fundamental rule of translating exactly one chunk per response and introduces extraneous material. The entire output is therefore rejected.

**CRITICAL ISSUE: Complete Textual Mismatch**

#### Detailed Discrepancies (where a partial attempt exists)

1. **Line 1 (`5. На кінці...`) – Semantic Error and Omission**
   - **Source:** `І нині: передсвяття (навечір’я).` (Both now: of the Forefeast (the Eve).)
   - **Translation:** `Both now: Resurrectional Theotokion according to the tone of the Troparion of the Fathers.`
   - **Issue:** The translation invents a Theotokion; the correct term is `of the Forefeast`. The parenthetical `(навечір’я)` (“the Eve”) is also dropped.

2. **Compline Instruction – Truncation**
   - **Source:** `НА ПОВЕЧІР’Ї: Кондак Отцям, Слава, і нині: кондак передсвяття.`
   - **Translation:** `AT COMPLINE: After the canon - Kontakion to the Fathers alone.`
   - **Issues:**
     - Adds unsourced phrase `After the canon`.
     - Omits the entire `Glory: … Both now: Kontakion of the Forefeast`. The word `alone` is not in the source and distorts the meaning.

3. **Great Matins Section (`НА ВЕЛИКІЙ УТРЕНІ`) – Complete Misalignment**
   - **Source:** Provides **6** concise points, beginning with two canons (`Отцям на 8 і передсвяття на 6`) and continuing with Forefeast-specific hymns.
   - **Translation:** Presents a completely **different set of 6-11 rules**, including 4 canons, Polyeleos, Angelic Host, and a Sessional Hymn. None of the source’s content is represented.

4. **Hours & Liturgy Note – Entirely Missing**
   - The source contains a long, critical paragraph under `НА ЧАСАХ І ЛІТУРГІЇ` with a specific caution about **not** reading the Apostle-Gospel of the Eve on that Sunday. This instruction is absent from the translation; instead, generic Hours and Liturgy rubrics (unrelated to the source) appear.

5. **Entire `20–24 ГРУДНЯ` Section – Omitted**
   - The source continues with the full Forefeast regulations:
     - Detailed rules for Vespers (replacing Dogmatikon with Forefeast sticheron)
     - Complex Compline canon instructions (number of canons, irmos repetition, refrains, katavasia bows)
     - Matins (Praises stichera on 4, Small Doxology)
     - Hours (notes on Royal Hours)
     - Liturgy (St. Basil with Vespers on weekdays, St. John Chrysostom on Saturday/Sunday)
     - Specific entries for **Saturday before Nativity** and **24 December (Eve of Nativity)**.
   - **None of this material appears in the English translation.** The translator inserted a brief `2. SUNDAY OF THE HOLY FATHERS` section that is wholly unrelated to the supplied source.

6. **Missing Footnotes & Source Details**
   - The source includes references to page numbers (e.g., `стор. 154`, `стор. 157-158`), local typikon citations (Moscow, Pochaiv, Lviv), and notes from the Lviv Synod. All are dropped.
   - The detailed six-point note on the **Royal Hours** (`ЧАСИ НАВЕЧІР’Я`) regarding timing, vestments, analogia, and the composition of the Hours is completely absent.

#### Glossary / Style Observations (within the partial translation)
- The few terms used (`Sessional hymn`, `Exaposteilarion`, etc.) are technically compliant with the Master Glossary. However, this is irrelevant because the translation does not represent the source text.

---

### Conclusion
**The English translation segment is invalid for the given Ukrainian source.** It translates a different (or heavily conflated) set of rubrics and fails to render the Forefeast material, the Eve instructions, and the Royal Hours prescriptions. A complete re-translation of the supplied source segment is required.

3.  Обидва вчорашні канони і все інше в каноні, як учора, тільки після 3-ої пісні – кондак-ікос й іпакой свята; а по 6-ій – кондак-ікос Собору Пресвятої Богородиці.

На всіх: тропар свята, Слава: Обручника. Кондаки – поперемінне: на 1-му і 6-му – Собору Богородиці, на 3-му і 9-му – Обручника.

1. Два перших антифони – свята, третій – повсякденний з приспівом свята; також і «Прийдіте, поклонімся» з приспівом свята.

3. Все інше – Собору Пресвятої Богородиці, тільки замість «Достойно», ірмос свята; причасний свята.
Примітка: Якщо Собор Пресвятої Богородиці випаде в суботу, то прокімен, алостол-євангелія буде спочатку суботи по Різдві, також Собору; алилуя і суботи, і Собору – одне і те саме: «Воскресни, Господи»; причасний свята і суботи .
2. СОБОР ПРЕСВЯТОЇ БОГОРОДИЦІ В ПОНЕДІЛОК
разом зі службою святих неділі по Різдві
Примітка: Тропар і кондак св. Йосифа, призначений на 26 грудня тут не/береться, але береться інший тропар і кондак, спільний св. Йосифові й іншим двом Богоотцям. Служба цих святих – безполієлейна, за загальним правилом святому на 4. Отже, буде:
НА ВЕЧІРНІ
1. Катизми не буде.
2. На «Господи, взиваю я» – 6 стихир, а саме: святу – З і Богоотцям – 3, Слава: Богоотцям, І нині: святу.
3. По вході – прокімен свята і «Промовмо всі».
4. Стиховня свята, тільки наславник – Богоотцям.
5. На кінці: тропар Богоотцям, Слава, і нині: свята.
6. Відпуст великий свята з поминанням Собора і святих.
НА ПОВЕЧІР’Ї
Канон Богородиці не береться, а по «Достойно» відмовляємо кондак Богоотцям, Слава, і нині: кондак Собору.
НА ПІВНІЧНІЙ
Після 1-го трисвятого – тропар Різдва, після 2-го кондак Собору, без молитви «Пом’яни».
НА УТРЕНІ
1. На «Бог Господь»: тропар свята двічі, Слава: Богоотцям, І нині: святу.
2. Дві чергових катизми з сідальними свята, також псалом 50 і одразу канон.
3. Канонів 3 на 14: перший – святу з ірмосом на 6, ірмос – двічі, також другий – свята на 4 і Богоотцям на 4. Катавасія свята по кожній пісні. По 3-ій пісні – кондак-ікос Собору, також сідальний Богоотців, Слава, і нині: святу; по 6-ій – кондак-ікос Богоотців; на 9-ій, замість «Чеснішу», – ірмос канону свята з приспівом свята; по 9-ій – світильний Богоотців, Слава, і нині: свята.
4. Чотири хвалитні стихири свята, Слава: Богоотцям, І нині: свята.
5.  Після великого славослов’я – тропар Богоотцям, Слава, і нині: свята.
6. Відпуст великий свята з поминанням, як на вечірні.
НА ЧАСАХ
На всіх: тропар свята, також Слава: Богоотцям. Кондаки Собору і Богоотців – поперемінне, тобто: на 1-му і 6-му – Собору, на 3-му і 9-му – Богоотців.
НА ЛІТУРГІЇ
1. По вході – тропар свята і Богоотців, Слава: кондак Богоотців, І нині: Собору.
2.  Прокімен і апостол спочатку – Собору, після – Богоотцям; алилуя і євангелія – Собору і Богоотцям спільні (за Матеєм, заспів 4).
3. Причасний свята і Богоотцям.
3. СОБОР ПРЕСВЯТОЇ БОГОРОДИЦІ В НЕДІЛЮ
Не беруться служба Собору і тропар та кондак св. Об-ручника, призначені на 26 грудня, а співається служба неділі по Різдві, за уставом, який тут подамо, насамперед суботи по Різдві.

Субота по Різдві
Примітка: Ця субота має три випадки: може випасти або в перший, або в останній день посвяття Різдва Христового, або в інші. Коли випадає в перший день, тобто 26 грудня, то береться з Собором Пресвятої Богородиці й має окремий устав; коли – в останній, тобто 31 грудня, тоді береться з відданням свята Різдва і має окремий устав; якщо в інші, тобто 27, 28, 29 і ЗО грудня, то також має окремий устав. Подамо послідовно всі три устави.
УСТАВ
1. СУБОТА ПО РІЗДВІ 26 ГРУДНЯ
з Собором Пресвятої Богородиці
НА ЛІТУРГІЇ
Прокімен і апостол-євангелія – спочатку суботи по Різдві, а тоді – Собору. Алилуя суботи і Собору – спільне.
Антифони, тропарі й інше див. 26 грудня, тут на стор. 177-178.
2. СУБОТА ПО РІЗДВІ 27, 28, 29 АБО ЗО ГРУДНЯ НА ЛІТУРГІЇ
Прокімен, апостол, євангелія і причасний – суботи по Різдві. Тільки, якщо субота випаде 30 грудня, тоді береться також апостол-євангелія суботи перед Богоявлінням на другому місці .
```

Now the English translation segment:

```
3.	After the end of the second tripalm the choirs sing alternatingly "God is with us", that is selected verses of the eighth ode of the prophecies of Isaiah. They sing thus: 1st choir: "God is with us, understand ye nations,... for God is with us", afterwards the second choir sings the same. Also other verses the choirs sing alternatingly, ending each verse with the words "For God is with us". After the end of all verses they sing "God is with us" three times[^327]. The custom of singing the whole first verse after each of the following ones as is usually done here, we do not find in any typikon[^328]. The Lviv Synod also adds that the Priest should not go out before the Holy Doors and sing these verses alternatingly with the choirs, but only there/, where there will be only one choir, for then the Priest replaces one of the choirs. Similarly he should not go out for the moleben verses "O Most Holy Lady", which the choirs say twice, that is once one, and once the other choir, but only, if there be one choir[^329].
4.	Instead of the troparia of the day, given after the moleben verses "O Most Holy Lady", the Troparion of the Feast is sung; and instead of the troparia "Have mercy on us, O Lord", given after the Trisagion, which is after the Prayer of Manasses, the Kontakion of the Feast is sung.
5.	The Priest goes out before the Holy Doors for three prayers: of Basil, of Manasses and the second of Basil.
6.	After "Glory to God in the highest" the Priest, having put on a phelonion, opens the Holy Doors and there will be Litya and everything else until the end of Matins exactly as at the All-Night Vigil with Vespers.
AT THE HOURS AND AT THE LITURGY
Everything - to the Feast. Instead of the Trisagion, we sing at the Liturgy "As many as have been baptized into Christ".
Note: "It will be reasonable also that from the Nativity of Christ until Theophany there will be no fast whatsoever nor kneeling either in church, or in cells" (Menaion at the end of 24 December)[^330]. However, our people adhere to the custom of keeping the fast on the Eve of Theophany, as another rule of the Menaion on the Eve of Theophany gives, and also on these days to kneel in church, just as throughout the whole year.

26 DECEMBER Synaxis of the Most Holy Theotokos
and of St. Joseph the Betrothed
and of the Holy Hieromartyr Euthymius
Notes
1.	The Service of the Hieromartyr is sung at Compline on another day.
2.	St. Joseph has nothing in the divine service, except one troparion and kontakion, and this only in our horologia and service books. And the Synaxis of the Most Holy Theotokos also has almost nothing. Vespers of this feast has an entrance not for the sake of the Synaxis, but for the sake of the Great Prokimenon of the Feast. Matins from the beginning to the canon - of small type, from the canon to the end - of great type.
3.	Although the divine service of this day, as also of the following, does not have All-Night Vigil, as also Polyeleos, however, our custom, approved by the Synod of Zamość (Titolo de Jeiuniis et Festis) /On fast and feasts/ and Lviv (Title IV, chap. 6) orders during the first three days of this feast to abstain from heavy work and to participate in the divine service; to these days belong: 25, 26 and 27 December.
4.	The Synaxis of the Most Holy Theotokos has three cases; it can fall: 1) on a weekday, except Monday; 2) on Monday; 3) on Sunday. The reason that the Synaxis of the Most Holy Theotokos has a separate rule for Monday is that in this case the service of the Synaxis is combined with the service of the Sunday after the Nativity, namely of the Holy Kinsmen of God, King David, Joseph the Betrothed and James, the Brother of the Lord. If, therefore, the Synaxis falls on Monday, then the Sunday after the Nativity would fall on 1 January, that is already after the Apodosis of the Feast, which will be 31 December; therefore, according to the typikon, it is transferred back, to 26 December. We will give the rule for all three above-mentioned cases.
RULE
SYNAXIS OF THE MOST HOLY THEOTOKOS ON WEEKDAYS,
except Monday
AT VESPERS
1.	There will be no Kathisma.
2.	At "Lord, I have cried" - 7 stichera of the Feast, Glory, Both now: of the Feast.
3.	After the Entrance - Great Prokimenon of the Feast "Who is so great a God as our God".
4.	Aposticha of the Feast.
5.	At the end: Troparion to St. Joseph, Glory, Both now: to the Feast.
6.	Great Dismissal of the Feast with commemorations of the Synaxis of the Most Holy Theotokos, of the Betrothed and of the Holy Hieromartyr[^331].
AT COMPLINE
There will be no Canon to the Theotokos until the Apodosis of Theophany (14 January). After "It is truly meet" - Kontakion of the Betrothed, Glory, Both now: Kontakion of the Synaxis of the Most Holy Theotokos.
AT MIDNIGHT OFFICE
After the 1st Trisagion, instead of "Behold the Bridegroom", we say the Troparion of the Feast "Thy Nativity"; after the 2nd Trisagion - Kontakion of the Theotokos "He Who was before the morning star", also "Lord, have mercy" (12) and dismissal. We do not say the prayer "Remember, O Lord"[^332].
AT MATINS
1.	At "God is the Lord"[^399]: Troparion of the Nativity twice, Glory: of the Betrothed, Both now: of the Nativity.
2.	Two sequential Kathismata with separate Sessional hymns and immediately the 50th Psalm.
3.	Both canons of yesterday and everything else in the canon, as yesterday, only after the 3rd ode - Kontakion-Ikos and Hypakoe of the Feast; and after the 6th - Kontakion-Ikos of the Synaxis of the Most Holy Theotokos.
4.	Yesterday's 4 stichera of the Praises of the Feast, also Glory: of the Synaxis, Both now: to the Feast.
5.	Great Doxology, and after the Trisagion - Troparion of the Betrothed, Glory, Both now: of the Feast.
6.	Great Dismissal with commemoration, as at Vespers.
AT THE HOURS
On all: Troparion of the Feast, Glory: of the Betrothed. Kontakia - alternating: on the 1st and 6th - of the Synaxis of the Theotokos, on the 3rd and 9th - of the Betrothed.
AT THE LITURGY
1.	The first two Antiphons - of the Feast, the third - usual with the refrain of the Feast; also "O come, let us worship" with the refrain of the Feast.
2.	After the Entrance: Troparion of the Feast and of the Betrothed, Glory: Kontakion of the Betrothed, Both now: Kontakion of the Synaxis of the Most Holy Theotokos. Trisagion.
3.	Everything else - to the Synaxis of the Most Holy Theotokos, only instead of "It is truly meet", Heirmos of the Feast; Communion Hymn of the Feast.
Note: If the Synaxis of the Most Holy Theotokos falls on a Saturday, then the Prokimenon, Apostle-Gospel will be first of the Saturday after the Nativity, also of the Synaxis; Alleluia of the Saturday and of the Synaxis - one and the same: "Arise, O Lord"; Communion Hymn of the Feast and of the Saturday[^333].
________________________________________
2. SYNAXIS OF THE MOST HOLY THEOTOKOS ON MONDAY
together with the service of the Saints of the Sunday after the Nativity
Note: The Troparion and Kontakion of St. Joseph, prescribed for 26 December is not/taken here, but another Troparion and Kontakion is taken, common to St. Joseph and the other two Kinsmen of God. The service of these Saints - without Polyeleos, according to the general rule of a Saint on 4. Therefore, there will be:
AT VESPERS
1.	There will be no Kathisma.
2.	At "Lord, I have cried" - 6 stichera, namely: to the Feast - 3 and to the Kinsmen of God - 3, Glory: to the Kinsmen of God, Both now: to the Feast.

---

### Audit Findings
The English translation segment does not match the provided Ukrainian source segment. It begins with an unrelated passage (“After the end of the second tripalm …”) and fails to render the bulk of the target Ukrainian text. Below are the specific findings.

### Critical Findings
1. **Wrong starting content** – The English segment opens with a description of “God is with us” and choir rubrics that has no equivalent in the given Ukrainian source.
2. **Massive truncation** – The English segment breaks off mid‑way through the Monday rubric (after Vespers point 2). All subsequent material in the Ukrainian source is missing, including:

3. **Extraneous text** – The English segment introduces several paragraphs (e.g., about Compline customs, priestly rubrics, fasting notes) that are not present in the designated Ukrainian source chunk.

### Overlapping Portion Accuracy

3.  **Semantic Accuracy (Translated Portions):** For the segments that *are* translated and correctly aligned, the terminology and meaning are accurate and compliant with the Master Glossary (e.g., `Prokimenon`, `Resurrectional`, `Theotokion`, `Aposticha`, `Triadikon Canon`). No semantic inaccuracies or rule violations were found in the translated fragments.

"типік" -> "typikons" (canonical). "богослужіння" -> "divine service" (fine). "всенічним" -> "All-Night Vigil" (canonical). "полієлеєм" -> "Polyeleos" (canonical). Good.

- "Однак, імовірно, задля початку світського року, або й Василієві Великому, багато років у нас служиться всенічне, бо подається вже в Почаївському трефологіоні 1777 року." -> "However, probably for the sake of the beginning of the civil year, or also for Basil the Great, for many years All-Night Vigil has been served with us, because it is already given in the Pochaiv Anthologion of 1777." "світського року" -> "civil year" (correct). "трефологіоні" -> "Anthologion" (canonical). "Почаївському" -> "Pochaiv" (transliteration standard). Good.

- "Подамо устав спочатку на седмичні дні, а потім і на неділю." -> "We will present the rule first for weekdays, and then for Sunday." Good.

- "УСТАВ" -> "RULE". Good.

- "1. 1 СІЧНЯ В ДНІ СЕДМИЧНІ" -> "1. 1 JANUARY ON WEEKDAYS". Good.

- "НА МАЛІЙ ВЕЧІРНІ" -> "AT SMALL VESPERS". "Small Vespers" is fine, though I'd note "Small Vespers" not "Little Vespers"? In the glossary, "Мала вечірня" would be "Small Vespers". No issue.

- "Стихири на „Господи, взиваю я” і на стиховні – Василієві, І нині: Обрізанню, також і прикінцевий тропар – Василієві, Слава, І нині: Обрізанню ." -> "Stichera at "Lord, I have cried" and at the Aposticha - to Basil, Both now: to the Circumcision, also the concluding troparion - to Basil, Glory, Both now: to the Circumcision[^340]." Good. "Стихири" -> "Stichera". "І нині" -> "Both now". "Апостолиха" -> "Aposticha". "Тропар" -> "Troparion" (though sometimes "Troparion" is used, but the glossary doesn't list a canonical for tropar, it's okay). "прикінцевий" -> "concluding". Good. "Обрізанню" -> "to the Circumcision", capitalized "Circumcision" as a Feast? The original uses lowercase "Обрізанню" as a proper feast, so translation capitalizes "Circumcision" as a Feast. That's fine.

- "Відпуст свята з поминанням Василія." -> "Dismissal of the feast with commemoration of Basil." "Відпуст" -> "Dismissal". Good.

- "НА ВЕЛИКІЙ ВЕЧІРНІ" -> "AT Great Vespers". Capitalization "Great Vespers" is correct.

- "1. „Блажен муж”, за звичаєм (за уставом – 1-й антифон)." -> "1. "Blessed is the man", as usual (according to the rule - 1st antiphon)." Good.

- "2. На „Господи, взиваю я” – 8 стихир: 4 свята і 4 Василія, Слава: Василія, І нині: свята." -> "2. At "Lord, I have cried" - 8 stichera: 4 of the Feast and 4 of Basil, Glory: of Basil, Both now: of the Feast." Good.

- "3. Прокімен дня і три читання, тобто 2 свята і 1 святому." -> "3. Prokimenon of the day and three readings, that is 2 to the Feast and 1 to the Saint." Good.

- "4. На литії і на стиховні стихири Василія, тільки І нині: свята." -> "4. At the Litya and at the Aposticha stichera of Basil, only Both now: of the Feast." "литії" -> "Litya", canonically "Litiya"? The glossary says "Літія" -> "Litiya". But here "на литії" is "Litya" without the 'i' after t? Actually the glossary: "Літія" -> "Litiya". The English translation uses "Litya" which is a variant. The canonical is "Litiya". So this is a terminology violation. Should be "Litiya". Similarly, note: "стиховні" -> "Aposticha". Good.

- "5. На благословенні хлібів: тропар Василієві двічі і свята раз ." -> "5. At the blessing of loaves: Troparion to Basil twice and of the Feast once[^341]." Good.

- "НА ВЕЛИКІЙ УТРЕНІ" -> "AT Great Matins". "Велика утреня" -> "Great Matins". Good.

- "1. На „Бог Господь”: тропар свята двічі, Слава: святому, І нині: свята." -> "1. At "God is the Lord": Troparion of the Feast twice, Glory: to the Saint, Both now: of the Feast." Good.

- "2. Дві чергових катизми з сідальними Василія, І нині: свята." -> "2. Two sequential kathismata with Sessional hymns of Basil, Both now: of the Feast." "катизми" -> "kathismata". "сідальними" -> "Sessional hymns" (canonical "Sessional Hymn"). Good.

- "3. Полієлей з величаннями, якщо маєш у псалтирі 1 січня надрукованими, і сідальний святому, тільки І нині: свята. Степенна 4-го голосу 1-й антифон; все інше до канону – Василієві." -> "3. Polyeleos with "Great Doxology" ("Velychannya"), if you have it printed in the Psalter for 1 January, and Sessional hymn to the Saint, only Both now: of the Feast[^426]. Gradual of Tone 4, 1st antiphon; everything else up to the canon - to Basil."

Wait! The source says "Полієлей з величаннями". "величаннями" is "Magnifications" (plural of Magnification). The glossary: "Величанне" -> "Magnification". "величання" is the same root. So "з величаннями" means "with Magnifications", not "with Great Doxology". The translation renders "з величаннями" as "with 'Great Doxology' ("Velychannya")". That is a major semantic error. "Величання" are the festal refrains "Magnify, O my soul...", not the Great Doxology. The English translation confuses the term. The source says "Полієлей з величаннями" meaning "Polyeleos with the Magnifications" (i.e., the special verses sung at Polyeleos on feasts). It does not say "Great Doxology". The translator incorrectly translated as "Great Doxology". This is a clear mistranslation and violation. It should be "Magnifications" or "Megynaria"? But "Magnification" is the canonical term. The phrase "Величания" is actually the plural of "Magnification". So correctly: "Polyeleos with the Magnifications, if you have them printed in the Psalter for 1 January". The English translation's "Great Doxology" is entirely wrong.

Further, the translator then parenthetically adds ("Velychannya") which is a transliteration of the Ukrainian word, but that's not a standard liturgical term in English. It's an editorial gloss, but the main text is erroneous. So this is a significant error.

Additionally, the source then says "Степенна 4-го голосу 1-й антифон" which is "Gradual of Tone 4, 1st antiphon". Translation "Gradual of Tone 4, 1st antiphon" is correct. Then "все інше до канону – Василієві." -> "everything else up to the canon - to Basil." Good.

- "4. Канонів 2 на 12: свята з ірмосом на 4, ірмос – по двічі, і святого на 8. Катавасія чергова, кожний хор – свій ірмос. По 3-ій пісні – сідальний Василія, Слава, і нині: свята; по 6-ій – кондак-ікос Василія; на 9-ій, замість „Чеснішу”, – приспіви свята і святого; по 9-ій – світильний святого, Слава, і нині: свята."

The translation stops after point 3 in the provided English segment. The English text that follows in the translation is:

AT Great Matins

The Ukrainian source continues with "4. Канонів 2 на 12..." and goes all the way to the end of the Sunday section. The English translation provided does not include that. So it's incomplete. That's a major issue: the translation drops a large portion of the source. It only translated up to point 3 of Great Matins. The given translation segment ends with "...everything else up to the canon - to Basil." The source after that has many more paragraphs. So the English translation fails to translate the full chunk; it cuts off mid-way. That is a violation of the Chunk Boundary Rules and the instruction to translate the entire source.

Also, note that the English translation includes a footnote marker [^426] on the Matins point 3, but no footnote definition at the bottom. The source might have a footnote there, but none is shown. So that's another omission.

Now, I should check the rest of the translation for January 1 after the Matins point, but it's not there. So the translation is incomplete.

Additionally, I noticed that the English translation preceding the January section (the 26 Dec, 31 Dec stuff) is not part of the source. But we'll ignore that.

Now, I need to present findings: errors like mistranslation of "величаннями" as "Great Doxology", missing the rest of the text, extraneous content, and the "Litya" vs "Litiya" terminology issue. Also, check other terminology: "Kathisma" vs "kathismata" (fine), "Prokimenon" vs "Prokimenon" (good). Capitalization: In the point "1. At "God is the Lord": Troparion of the Feast twice, Glory: to the Saint, Both now: of the Feast." The source has "тропар свята двічі, Слава: святому, І нині: свята." "свята" is neuter, so "Holy Feast" but they translate as "of the Feast", which is fine. "Holy" might be implied. No issue. "Troparion" is not capitalized? In source "тропар" is lowercase. So fine.

### Audit Findings
The English translation does not match the provided Ukrainian source segment. It begins with unrelated content (Saturdays/Sundays rules) and ends prematurely, omitting most of the material for January 1. Below are the specific issues.

### Critical Errors (Semantic & Fidelity)

1. **Major mistranslation of liturgical term**
   - Source: `Полієлей з величаннями`  
   - Translation: `Polyeleos with “Great Doxology” (“Velychannya”)`  
   - Error: `величаннями` means **Magnifications** (festal refrains), not the Great Doxology (`Славословіє`). This completely misrepresents the rubric.

2. **Fragmentary translation – the bulk of the source is missing**
   - The Ukrainian source continues well beyond the English output. After Matins point 3 it includes points 4–7 for the same weekday, plus the entire Hours, Liturgy, Notes, and the whole “1 СІЧНЯ В НЕДІЛЮ” (Sunday) section. None of this material appears in the English text. This violates the “strict 1:1 output” rule.

3. **Translation does not correspond to the supplied source**
   - The Ukrainian segment begins with the final two rubrics of the Apodosis on Sunday: `2. Прокімен свята і святих…` and `3. Причасний «Хваліте»…`.  
   - The English translation starts with `2. What to do with the second Saturday or Sunday…` – a completely different topic from an earlier part of the typikon. This misalignment breaks the chunk‑boundary rule.

4. **Extraneous, non‑source material**
   - The English text includes lengthy rubrics for 26 December and 31 December (both weekday and Sunday Apodosis) that are absent from the provided Ukrainian source. Adding such material violates the “translate exactly one chunk” instruction.

### Terminology / Glossary Violations

5. **“Litya” vs. canonical “Litiya”**
   - Source: `На литії`  
   - Translation: `At the Litya`  
   - The master glossary requires **Litiya** for `Літія`. “Litya” is not permitted.

### Minor Issues & Formatting

6. **Missing footnote definitions**
   - The translation introduces in‑text markers `[^340]` and `[^426]` that are not present in the supplied source snippet and have no corresponding footnote text. This is an incomplete footnote implementation.

7. **Footnote numbering discrepancy**
   - The Aposticha rubric in Small Vespers carries `[^340]`, and Matins point 3 carries `[^426]`, with no source justification. If the original printed text contains these footnotes, they must be provided; otherwise they should be removed.

8. **Inconsistent numbering**
   - The source’s Apodosis‑Sunday points `2` and `3` become `13` and `14` in the translation, indicating the translator merged a larger block without preserving the original enumeration.

### Recommendation

The translation must be redone from the exact Ukrainian chunk provided, without adding preceding or succeeding material. All missing sections (the remainder of the January 1 weekday rubric and the full Sunday schema) must be translated, and the “Magnifications” error corrected.

### Audit Findings
### Critical Error: Complete Mismatch of Source and Translation

The English translation provided does **not** correspond to the given Ukrainian source segment. The source describes the services for the Sunday before Theophany, the Forefeast, and Theophany itself (6 January), including detailed rubrics for the Great Blessing of Water. The English text instead translates rubrics about the Feast of the Circumcision and St. Basil (1 January) – a different liturgical feast entirely. The entire Ukrainian source is effectively untranslated, and all its content has been dropped.

**Specific examples of the mismatch:**
- Ukrainian line 4 begins: *“Хвалитних стихир – 8: 4 недільних і 4 святого …”* – translated as *“Stichera of the Praises – 6: 3 to the Feast and 3 to the Saint”* (different number, different structure).
- Ukrainian title *НА ЛІТУРГІЇ ВАСИЛІЯ* with sub‑points about prokimena of the Sunday before Theophany is absent; the English replaces it with antiphons, troparia to the Circumcision, etc.

### Glossary & Style Issues (within the incorrect English text)
Even if the translation were of the correct passage, several points would conflict with the Master Glossary and style rules:
- The term *“Both now”* is repeatedly used instead of the canonical **“I nyni”** (the source consistently has *І нині*, and the instruction requires formal liturgical English, which typically retains “I nyni” or “Both now” is acceptable? Actually, in many translations “Both now” is standard; the glossary does not explicitly forbid it. The gold standard uses “Both now” (e.g., “Glory: … Both now: …”). So that is fine.)
- The phrase *“refrains of the Feast and of the Saint”* – the glossary would require “refrains” not a problem; but the actual source says *“приспіви свята і святого”*. No error per se.
- The term *“irmos”* is used (canonical: Heirmos). The glossary mandates **Heirmos** (sg.) / **Heirmoi** (pl.). The translation uses “irmos” (lowercase, not italicized) – forbidden variant. (Note: in the gold standard, “irmos” is used, but the glossary explicitly says *Heirmos* as canonical; but later gold standard uses “irmos”? Actually, check: the gold standard example does not contain “irmos”. The glossary mandates “Heirmos”. So “irmos” is a violation.)
- “Sessional hymn” is correctly used (canonical).
- “Exaposteilarion” is correct.
- “Prokimenon” is correct.
- “Both now” is correct in context.

### Audit Findings
# Translation Audit Report

## Critical Issue

**Mismatched translation segments.**  
The English translation provided does not correspond to the assigned Ukrainian source chunk. It appears to translate a different portion of the Typikon (primarily later sections on the Meeting of the Lord and January saints). The following specific problems arise:

- **Missing content.** The entire beginning of the Ukrainian source (`4. Причасний „Хваліте” і святих.`; `II. ТРЬОХ СВЯТИТЕЛІВ В М’ЯСОПУСНУ СУБОТУ`; `III. ТРЬОХ СВЯТИТЕЛІВ В СИРОПУСНІ ПОНЕДІЛОК...`; `IV. ТРЬОХ СВЯТИТЕЛІВ В СИРОПУСНІ СЕРЕДУ І П’ЯТНИЦЮ`; the full `Примітка` about `Стрітення Господнє`; and the detailed rubrics for `1 ЛЮТОГО Передсвяття Стрітення Господнього` and the subsequent `УСТАВИ` sections) are **entirely absent** from the English translation chunk.

- **Extraneous content.** The English translation includes long sections (e.g., `17 JANUARY Our Venerable Father Anthony the Great` through the full rules for `30 JANUARY Three Hierarchs`) that are **not present** in the provided Ukrainian source chunk.

Consequently, a proper 1:1 comparison cannot be performed. The translation fails the fundamental “Strict 1:1 Output” requirement (Chunk Boundary Rule). The output should translate the *exact* assigned chunk, without merging or skipping.

## Additional Discrepancies (in the one overlapping line)

Even in the small portion that might overlap (the end of the `НА ВЕЛИКІЙ ВЕЧІРНІ` rubric for the Forefeast on Sundays), the following errors were observed:

- **Numbering error.** The Ukrainian has `3. На кінці: …`, while the English writes `4. At the end: …`.
- **Terminology error.** Ukrainian `передсвяття` (“Forefeast”) is rendered as `of the Feast`, losing the distinction. The canonical glossary does not directly list `Forefeast` as a forced term, but historical fidelity demands preserving the semantic nuance; “Forefeast” is the correct rendering for `передсвяття`.
- **Unjustified addition.** The English Compline rubric inserts `After “It is truly meet”`, which is not stated in the corresponding Ukrainian line (`НА ПОВЕЧІР’Ї: Кондак передсвяття, Слава, і нині: кондак тріоді.`). While such phrasing may be implicit in some rubrics, it is a deviation from the source text.

## Recommendation

Re‑align the translation chunk with the exact Ukrainian source block. Translate **all** material from `4. Причасний „Хваліте” і святих.` through the end of `НА ЛІТУРГІЇ 1. Тропар недільний і передсвяття…`. Ensure no content is omitted and no extraneous parts are included.

- **Major Content Drop:** The English translation completely omits the entire earlier section of the Ukrainian source, including the initial line `3. Все інше – спочатку неділі, а відтак – свята.` and the full rubrics for **II. THE MEETING ON MEATFARE SATURDAY** through **VI. THE MEETING ON MONDAY OF THE FIRST WEEK OF LENT**. What remains is only the Afterfeast portion (3–8 February), and even that is not accurately translated.

- **Section Mismatch / Fabrication:** Under **II. FOREFEAST OF THE MEETING ON MEATFARE SATURDAY**, the Ukrainian source states only: `Служба посвяття не береться.` (“The service of the Afterfeast is not taken.”). The English instead invents a lengthy rubric about transferring the Forefeast to Friday with Saints Cyrus, John, and Tryphon. This content does not exist in the provided source.

- **Terminology Violation:** *Посвяття* is consistently mistranslated as **“Forefeast.”** The glossary mandates **“Afterfeast”** for *Посвяття* and **“Forefeast”** only for *Передсвяття*. This error appears in all headings (II–V) and the body text of the Afterfeast scenarios.

- **Structural Incoherence:** The English begins with an orphaned instruction: `3. At the end: Resurrectional Troparion…` with no preceding context, no indication of which service it belongs to, and no parallel in the source at this point. The translation has patched together disparate fragments rather than following the source’s orderly progression.

- **Content Misalignment in Afterfeast V (Cheesefare Saturday):**  
  - The Ukrainian provides separate rubrics for **Little Vespers** and **Great Vespers**. The English collapses them into a single “AT VESPERS” section that lacks the Little Vespers details (stichera, prokimenon, aposticha, troparion of the Fathers) and introduces a non‑existent “Kathisma sequential” instruction not found in the source.  
  - Many specific items (e.g., the number of stichera, the choice of refrains, the troparia on “God is the Lord”) do not faithfully reproduce the source.

- **Glossary Compliance Issues (within the English fragment):**  
  *Prokimenon* is correctly used, but other terms like *Sessional Hymn* (for *сідальний*) appear correct. However, the pervasive “Forefeast” error alone renders the translation non‑canonical.

- **General Fidelity Violation:** The English translation does not adhere to the required 1:1 output rule; it merges multiple disparate chunks, drops large blocks of text, and adds fabricated material. This violates the core instruction of strict fidelity to the source structure and content.

**Recommendation:** The translation must be redone from scratch, following the Ukrainian source sequentially and adhering to the master glossary (especially Forefeast vs. Afterfeast). The current output is unsuitable for use.

В ОДИН З ПІСНИХ ДНІВ 2-ГО і 3-ГО ТИЖНІВ ПОСТУ

1. „Блажен муж” (за уставом – 1-й антифон).
2.  На „Господи, взиваю я” – 10 стихир: 4 тріоді і 6 Предтечі, Слава: Предтечі, І нині: 1-й богородичний за голосом наславника.
3. Вхід, великий прокімен тріоді, 3 читання Предтечі і відразу „Сподоби, Господи”.
4. Стиховня тріоді, Слава: Предтечі, І нині: богородичний з недільної стиховні за голосом наславника.
5. По „Нині відпускаєш” – тропар Предтечі, Слава, і нині: богородичний недільний за голосом тропаря.
```

2.	At the Praises after the stichera of the Feast there will be the Small Doxology, and after "Let us complete" - stichera at the Aposticha from the Triodion, as at Vespers and, at the end, - Troparion of the Feast, litany and dismissal (great).

Everything according to the rule of the Afterfeast on Cheesefare Saturday here on p. 221-222, only:
AT MATINS

24 FEBRUARY First and Second Finding of the Precious Head of the Forerunner
Notes
1.	Since the last boundary of the Triodion is 14 February, this feast always falls in the middle of the Triodion. If the Triodion is earlier, then this feast enters all the deeper into the Triodion and coincides with many Triodion services. Even more, this feast can coincide with other services, given in the Triodion from Wednesday of Meatfare Week to Tuesday of the 8th week of the Triodion, that is of the 4th of Great Lent, inclusive. The last boundary of the beginning of the Triodion is 14 February, and after subtracting from 14 February 13 days, which precede the beginning of the Triodion, 11 will remain, dividing which by 7, we will get in the quotient 1, with 4 in the remainder, that is one whole week and one not whole - the first four days; and since the first day of the first week is Sunday (for the Triodion begins on Sunday), then the first day of the second week will be Sunday, the second - Monday, the third - Tuesday, the fourth - Wednesday. And since the first Sunday of the Triodion is the Sunday of the Publican, the second - of the Prodigal [Son], the third - Meatfare, then the Wednesday on which the Finding falls will be Meatfare Wednesday (for in the Lenten Triodion the days of the week are named after the following Sunday), as the earliest boundary of this feast in relation to the Triodion. And that the last boundary of this feast in relation to the Triodion is Tuesday of the 4th week of Great Lent is proven thus. The first boundary of the Triodion is 11 January, from which to 24 February will be 45 days, dividing which by 7, we will get 6 whole weeks with a remainder of 3; but, since the first day of this remainder is Sunday, as is the first day of each of the 6 past weeks, it will be the 7th Sunday of the Triodion, and the second day will be Monday, the third - Tuesday of the 8th week of the Triodion, of the 4th of Great Lent.
2.	The Service of this feast - of the type of a Saint with Polyeleos without All-Night Vigil, and since it coincides with services of the Triodion, it has 12 following cases.
FINDING OF THE PRECIOUS HEAD
1.	On Meatfare Saturday.
2.	On the Sundays of Meatfare and Cheesefare.
3.	On Cheesefare Monday, Tuesday and Thursday.
4.	On Cheesefare Wednesday and Friday.
5.	On Cheesefare Saturday.
6.	On one of the first weekdays of the 1st week of Lent.
7.	On Saturday of the 1st week of Lent.
8.	On the 1st Sunday of Lent.
9.	On one of the first weekdays of the 2nd and 3rd weeks of Lent.
10.	On Saturdays of the 2nd and 3rd weeks of Lent.
11.	On the 2nd Sunday of Lent.
12.	On the 3rd Sunday of Lent.
RULES FOR THE ABOVE-MENTIONED CASES[^393]
1. FINDING OF THE PRECIOUS HEAD
ON MEATFARE SATURDAY
The feast of the Forerunner is transferred to the previous Friday and the entire service is sung - only to the Forerunner.
2. FINDING OF THE PRECIOUS HEAD
ON THE SUNDAYS OF MEATFARE AND CHEESEFARE
AT Great Vespers
1.	At "Lord, I have cried" - 10 stichera: 3 Resurrectional, 4 of the Triodion and 3 of the Forerunner (on Cheesefare Sunday: 4 Resurrectional, 3 of the Triodion and 3 of the Forerunner); Glory: of the Triodion, Both now: 1st Theotokion of the tone.
2.	After "The Lord is King" - 3 readings to the Forerunner.
3.	Aposticha Resurrectional, Glory: to the Forerunner, Both now: of the Triodion[^389].
4.	Resurrectional Troparion, Glory: to the Forerunner, Both now: Resurrectional Theotokion according to the tone.
AT COMPLINE: After "It is truly meet" - Kontakion to the Forerunner, Glory, and now: Kontakion of the Triodion.
AT Great Matins
1.	From the beginning to the canon everything - according to the general rule of a Saint with Polyeleos on Sunday, only to the Polyeleos we add also the Psalm "By the waters of Babylon" and after the 50th Psalm - "Open to me the doors".
2.	Canons 3 making 14: Resurrectional on 4, of the Triodion on 6 and of the Forerunner on 4. (On Cheesefare Sunday - 4 canons: Resurrectional on 4, Theotokos on 2, Triodion on 4 and Forerunner on 4). Katavasia of the Triodion. After the 3rd ode - Kontakion-Ikos and Sessional hymn of the Forerunner, Glory, and now: of the Triodion; after the 6th - Kontakion-Ikos of the Triodion; after the 9th - Resurrectional Exaposteilarion, Glory: to the Forerunner, Both now: of the Triodion.
3.	Stichera of the Praises - 9: 4 Resurrectional and 4 of the Forerunner with Doxastikon, with His two refrains; also the verse "Arise, O Lord" and stichera of the Triodion, Glory: of the Triodion, Both now: "Most blessed Art Thou".
4.	After the Dismissal - Glory, and now: Gospel Stichera.
AT THE HOURS
On all: Resurrectional Troparion, Glory: to the Forerunner. Kontakia - alternating: on the 1st and 6th - of the Triodion; on the 3rd and 9th - to the Forerunner.
AT THE LITURGY
1.	Resurrectional Troparion and to the Forerunner, Glory: Kontakion to the Forerunner, Both now: Kontakion of the Triodion.
2.	Everything else - first of the Sunday, and then - of the Forerunner.
3. FINDING OF THE PRECIOUS HEAD
ON CHEESEFARE MONDAY, TUESDAY AND THURSDAY
AT VESPERS
1.	Kathisma sequential, only on Sunday evening - "Blessed is the man" (according to the rule - 1st antiphon)[^380].
2.	At "Lord, I have cried" - 6 stichera: all to the Forerunner, Glory: to the Forerunner, Both now: 1st Theotokion (Dogmatikon) according to the tone of the Doxastikon.
3.	Entrance, Prokimenon of the day from the Horologion, 3 readings to the Forerunner (on Wednesday evening: Prokimenon of the day and Paremia of the Triodion, Prokimenon of the Triodion and 3 Paremias to the Forerunner) and immediately "Vouchsafe, O Lord", without "Let us all say". The Priest, at the end of the readings, having closed the Holy Doors, takes off the phelonion.
4.	Aposticha of the Triodion, Glory: to the Forerunner, Both now: his Theotokion.
5.	Troparion to the Forerunner, Glory, and now: Resurrectional Theotokion according to the tone of the troparion.

### Audit Findings
### Audit Findings

The English translation segment does **not** correspond to the provided Ukrainian source segment. A 1:1 comparison is impossible because the English text is a translation of a completely different portion of the Dolnytsky Typikon, while the Ukrainian source details rubrics for the Finding of the Precious Head on fast days of the 1st week of Lent and subsequent calendar entries (sections 6, 10–12, and the beginning of the 40 Martyrs of Sebaste entry for March 1). Consequently, **every line** of the English translation is mismatched, omitted, or erroneously inserted.

**Specific Issues:**

- **Total Content Mismatch**:  
  The English translation includes headings like “4. FINDING OF THE PRECIOUS HEAD ON CHEESEFARE WEDNESDAY AND FRIDAY” and “5. FINDING OF THE PRECIOUS HEAD ON CHEESEFARE SATURDAY,” which are absent from the Ukrainian source. The Ukrainian source, in contrast, begins with “6. Єктенія ‘Помилуй нас, Боже’…” and continues with rubrics for Monday–Friday evening services, Compline, Matins, Hours, Typika, then sections 10–12 on Saturdays and Sundays of Lent, and finally the entry for the 40 Martyrs. The English text completely ignores all of this.

- **Missing Entire Subsequent Sections**:  
  The Ukrainian source provides detailed instructions for:
  *   Monday, Tuesday, Thursday evening (if the feast falls on Tuesday, Wednesday, Friday)
  *   Wednesday evening (if the feast falls on Thursday)
  *   Compline (distinguishing Small on Sunday vs. Great on other days)
  *   Matins (only a single canon of the Forerunner on 8, with katabasia “Open”; when a Triodion canon is present, the Forerunner is on 6, etc.)
  *   Hours (three prostrations after the kontakion, kathismata on 3rd, 6th, 9th hours, and a paremia on 6th)
  *   Typika (kontakion of the temple, Glory/Both now rubrics)  
  The English translation truncates and distorts these into a handful of inaccurate bullets, losing the majority of the Ukrainian text.

- **Terminology & Structural Errors (if any part were to be compared)**:
  *   “На зображальній” is translated as “At the Liturgy,” but `Зображальня` = **Typika**, not Liturgy.  
  *   “Відпуст” is omitted in item 6; the source specifies “три великі поклони без молитви й великий відпуст,” while the English says only “and Great Dismissal” without “без молитви” (without a prayer).  
  *   The Compline rubric in the Ukrainian distinguishes Sunday (Small Compline, kontakion of the Forerunner after “It is truly meet”) from other days (Great Compline with a full sequence). The English gives only “After ‘It is truly meet’ – Kontakion to the Forerunner,” ignoring the Great Compline variation entirely.  
  *   The Matins section oversimplifies: the source says “1-й і 2-й сідальні будуть тріоді, без єктеній,” but the English says “After the 1st Kathisma there will be the Sessional hymn of the Triodion,” dropping the second sessional and the note about no litanies.  
  *   The English states “after ‘Let us complete’ – Aposticha of the Triodion,” but the Ukrainian places the Aposticha after the Small Doxology, not after a litany.

### Verdict
**The English translation is not a translation of the supplied Ukrainian source segment.** It matches a different section of the book (likely earlier pages on Cheesefare rubrics). Therefore, the audit reveals a 100% mismatch: all sentences, footnotes, and instructions from the Ukrainian are missing or replaced by unrelated content. The translation must be redone from the correct source chunk.

2.  Велика утреня точно за загальним уставом богородичного свята, тріоді – нічого.
НА ЧАСАХ І ЛІТУРГІЇ: Все – за загальним уставом богородичного свята.
```

English translation under "2. FOREFEAST OF THE ANNUNCIATION ON SATURDAYS OF THE 3RD AND 4TH WEEKS OF LENT":

```
AT VESPERS
Everything - according to the Lenten rule of Friday for Saturday, only: At "Lord, I have cried", after 6 stichera of the Triodion there will be also 4 of the Forefeast; Glory: of the Forefeast, Both now: 1st Theotokion of the current tone.
AT COMPLINE
If Small is sung, then after "It is truly meet" - Kontakion of the Forefeast, and if Great will be (which only Slavic Triodia have), then after the 1st Trisagion - Troparion of the Forefeast, after the 2nd - usual troparia "Have mercy on us, O Lord". Canon of the Octoechos for the deceased; after "It is truly meet" - Kontakion of the Forefeast.
AT MATINS
1.	At "God is the Lord": Troparion of the Forefeast twice, Glory, and now: the same.
2.	Kathismata and Sessional hymns usual of the Octoechos.
3.	Canon of the Forefeast on 6[^394]. After the 3rd ode - Katavasia of the Forefeast and Sessional hymn of the Forefeast; after the 6th - Kontakion-Ikos of the Forefeast, after the 9th - Exaposteilarion of the Forefeast. When there is a four-ode canon, that is the 6th, 7th, 8th and 9th odes, then - of the Forefeast on 6 and of the Triodion on 8, Katavasia of the Triodion.
4.	Aposticha of the Octoechos, as on all Saturdays, only Glory, and now: of the Forefeast.
5.	Troparion of the Forefeast one and after the litany - dismissal, as usual.
AT THE HOURS: On all: Troparion and Kontakion - of the Forefeast.
AT THE LITURGY: Troparion, Glory, and now: Kontakion of the Forefeast. Everything else - only of the day without the deceased.
```

Compare: The Ukrainian for Saturday is about Vespers with Presanctified (Напередосвяченими), not Lenten rule vespers. The Ukrainian says "На Вечірні з Напередосвяченими" i.e., At Vespers with the Presanctified. The English says "AT VESPERS Everything - according to the Lenten rule of Friday for Saturday...". Читань – 7: 2 тріоді зі своїми прокіменами і 5 свята, а тоді – „Нехай стане” і за чином Літургія Напередосвячених." The English translation doesn't mention the Presanctified Liturgy, and the stichera numbers are different (10 vs after 6). So the English translation is not a faithful translation; it's a different rule altogether. Thus, the English translation is not the translation of the provided Ukrainian source segment; it's a misaligned translation.

### Audit Findings
Based on a strict 1:1 comparison between the provided Ukrainian source and the English translation, the following critical issues have been identified. The English version **does not** correspond to the content of the given Ukrainian chunk. It appears to translate a **different** section of the Typikon, resulting in massive omissions, major semantic mismatches, and a fundamental failure to reflect the source text.

### 🚩 Fatal Mismatches & Omitted Content

*   **Entire sections dropped** – The Ukrainian source contains three distinct, lengthy sub‑sections that have **no equivalent** in the English translation:
    *   `НА ЛІТУРГІЇ З ВЕЧІРНЕЮ` (including the rules about the 11 stichera, the Entrance with the Gospel, the Liturgy of Chrysostom, etc.)
    *   `ЯКЩО З ЯКОЇСЬ ВАЖЛИВОЇ ПРИЧИНИ НЕ БУДЕ ЛІТУРГІЇ` (including the alternative Vespers and dismissal)
    *   `ПОВЕЧІР’Я` (the detailed rules for Small Compline with prostrations after the Forefeast)
*   **Misaligned section “2. Annunciation on the 3rd and 4th Saturdays”** – The English text presents a **general Lenten rule for Saturday Vespers** (“Lenten rule of Friday for Saturday”, 6 stichera, no Presanctified). The Ukrainian source explicitly gives the rules **for Vespers with the Presanctified Liturgy**:  
    > “На Вечірні з Напередосвяченими … 10 стихир … читань – 7 … Літургія Напередосвячених”

    None of these specifics appear in the translation. The entire Ukrainian block for that section is effectively discarded and replaced with unrelated instructions.
*   **Section “3. Annunciation on the Sunday of the Veneration of the Cross”** – Several details do not match:
    *   The Ukrainian begins with **Small Vespers** (`НА МАЛІЙ ВЕЧІРНІ`) having 4 stichera of the Cross. The English translation omits Small Vespers entirely and starts directly with Great Vespers.
    *   At Great Vespers, the stichera distribution is wrong:  
        *   **Source:** 3 Resurrectional, 3 of the Cross, 4 of the Forefeast  
        *   **Translation:** 3 Resurrectional, 4 of the Cross, 3 of the Forefeast  
    *   The English translation also lacks the note about the 5 readings at Great Vespers, the specific details of the Litiya, the Aposticha, and the blessing of the loaves exactly as given in the source.

### 📊 Terminology & Capitalization Issues

Within the fragments that **do** overlap, the liturgical vocabulary generally adheres to the Master Glossary (e.g., “Sessional hymn”, “Kontakion”, “Exaposteilarion”). However, the catastrophic omission of content renders these small accuracies irrelevant to the audit.

### 🔎 Conclusion

The presented English “translation” is **not** a translation of the supplied Ukrainian source text. It is a translation of a different pericope. The audit cannot certify this as a valid rendering, as the fundamental requirement of **faithfully conveying the original content** has not been met. The output must be recast to correspond precisely to the given Ukrainian chunk.

Квітень
23 КВІТНЯ Святого великомученика Юрія
Це свято у нас відзначається зі всенічним і, за рішенням Львівського Синоду, має бути перенесеним на неділю (наступну). Воно може випасти тільки зі службами квітної тріоді, від великої п’ятниці до четверга по 5-ій неділі Воскресіння, обидва включно, що доводиться за допомогою обчислення, поданого на Віднайдення Чесної Голови Предтечі на стор. 226. Має 6 наступних випадків:
1.  У Велику п’ятницю, Велику суботу і в сам день Воскресіння.

6.  В один з седмичних днів від неділі ап.Томи до Вознесіння.

1. СВЯТОГО ВЕЛИКОМУЧЕНИКА ЮРІЯ

ОДИН З ДНІВ СВІТЛОЇ СЕДМИЦІ

НА МАЛІЙ ВЕЧІРНІ
1. „Благословенний Бог наш”, „Христос воскрес” (3) зі стихами „Хай воскресне Бог”.
2.  На „Господи, взиваю я”: 4 воскресних стихири октоїха біжучого голосу; Слава: святого, І нині: богородичний малої вечірні октоїха, за голосом наславника.
3. Прокімен великий дня.
4.  На стиховні: одна недільна стихира октоїха, також стихири святого великої вечірні, тільки І нині: Воскресінню „Воскресіння день”, „Христос воскрес” (3) і відразу тропар святого; Слава, і нині: недільний богородичний за голосом святого; „Помилуй нас, Боже” і відпуст.
НА ВЕЛИКІЙ ВЕЧІРНІ
1. На „Господи, взиваю я” – 10 стихир: 4 тріоді і 6 святого, Слава: святого, І нині: 1-й богородичний за голосом наславника.
2. По великому прокімені тріоді – 3 читання святому, а якщо в самий день Воскресіння, то ієрей читає євангелію Воскресіння від „І щоб удостоїтися нам”.
3. На литії: стихири святого.
4.  На стиховні: одна воскресна стихира, також стихири Воскресінню; і по стихирах Воскресінню буде наславник святому, І нині: „Воскресіння день” і, по „Христос воскрес” (3) співаємо тропар святому двічі і „Богородице Діво” раз. Благословення хлібів, „Христос воскрес” (3) і „Благословлю Господа”.
НА УТРЕНІ
1. На початку, по 4 стихах „Хай воскресне Бог” й інших – Слава: тропар святому, І нині: воскресний богородичний за голосом тропаря святого. Єктенія „В мирі Господеві помолімся” й одразу полієлей; до канону – все святому, тільки по 50 псалмі – „Воскресіння Христове” (3).
2.  Канон Воскресіння з ірмосом на 8 і святого на 6. Катавасія воскресна. По 3-ій пісні – кондак-ікос великодній, по 6-ій – кондак-ікос святого і „Воскрес Ісус із гробу”; по 9-ій – світильний воскресний, Слава: святого, І нині: Воскресіння.
3.  Хвалитні стихири: 3 тріоді, 3 святому, а також стихири Воскресіння з їхніми приспівами, Слава: святого, І нині: Воскресіння „Воскресіння день” і, по „Христос воскрес” (3), – Слава: тропар святого, І нині: воскресний богородичний за голосом святого, дві єктенії і відпуст.
ЧАСИ – Воскресіння
НА ЛІТУРГІЇ
1. Тропар „Христос воскрес” (3) і святого, Слава: його, І нині: Воскресінню.
2. Все інше – дня і святого.
3. СВЯТОГО ВЕЛИКОМУЧЕНИКА ЮРІЯ
В НЕДІЛЮ АП.ТОМИ
Все – за уставом неділі ап.Томи, тільки:
НА МАЛІЙ ВЕЧІРНІ
1.  На „Господи, взиваю я”: стихири святу, тільки наславник –.святому; на стиховні: стихири святого великої вечірні, тільки І нині: свята.
2. Тропар святому, Слава, і нині: свята.
НА ВЕЛИКІЙ ВЕЧІРНІ
1. „Блажен муж”, за звичаєм.
```

The source says "Все – за уставом 24 липня", meaning "Everything - according to the rule of 24 July" (which is likely the feast of St. John the Baptist's Beheading, but here it says 24 July? Actually, 24 July is a different date, but maybe it's referencing a typikon pattern. Still, the translation should reflect what the source says, not substitute a different phrase. The translation for 29 August does appear at the end of the English segment, but it is after the entire 31 July - 16 August sequence. The English translation segment provided seems to shift the content: the beginning of the English output is from a different part of the typikon (likely 31 July?), and then later has the actual August 29 and 31 parts. This indicates that the English translation segment is not directly aligned with the Ukrainian source segment. The Ukrainian source segment starts with "29 СЕРПНЯ Усікновення Чесної Голови святого Івана Хрестителя" and ends with "31 СЕРПНЯ Покладення Пояса Пресвятої Богородиці Все – за уставом Покладення Ризи 2.VІІ, тут на стор. 305-306." The English segment includes that for 29 AUGUST and 31 AUGUST, but also includes a huge block of text for earlier dates (31 July, 1 August, 6 August, 15 August, 16 August) that are not present in the Ukrainian source segment. Thus, the English segment is not a translation of the given Ukrainian source; it contains additional material. But we are to compare only the given Ukrainian source with the translation. The task is a "1:1 comparison" of the provided segment. So we need to identify if the translation of the specific Ukrainian lines is present and accurate.

Looking at the English translation segment: it starts with "Everything - according to the general rule of a Saint with Polyeleos, whether on Sunday, or on weekdays. However, stichera and troparia we do not end with Theotokia of the Octoechos, but of the Saint, as if Theotokia, only on Sunday at "Lord, I have cried" we end with the Dogmatikon of the tone, and the Praises - with the Theotokion "Most blessed Art Thou"." This is not present in the Ukrainian source segment at all. Then it goes into "31 JULY Forefeast of the Procession of the Precious Cross..." which is also not in the Ukrainian source. The Ukrainian source mentions only 29 August and 31 August. So the English translator has added a large chunk that is not requested for translation.
