Then "31 AUGUST Deposition of the Sash of the Most Holy Theotokos" translates the 31 August entry. So the relevant translation matching the source is only the last two sections. However, the initial part of the English output is unrelated to the source. That might be a chunking mistake; the translator might have output a larger block that includes prior pages. But in auditing, we compare the source lines with the translation lines for those dates.

Now examine the translation for 29 August:
English: "29 AUGUST Beheading of the Precious Head of St. John the Baptist
Everything - according to the rule of 24 June, however, by the decision of the Lviv Synod, must be transferred from a weekday to Sunday with All-Night Vigil. It is usually transferred to the following Sunday, only if the following Sunday falls on 1 September, then the service is transferred to the previous Sunday, so as not to coincide with three other services, that is Resurrectional, of the Indiction and of St. Simeon[^464]. The fast of the Beheading we do not transfer to Sunday, but keep on the very day of the feast[^465]."

Compare with Ukrainian source: "29 СЕРПНЯ Усікновення Чесної Голови святого Івана Хрестителя
Все – за уставом 24 липня, одначе, за рішенням Львівського Синоду, має бути перенесена з дня седмичного на неділю зі всенічним. Переноситься звичайно на наступну неділю, тільки якщо наступна неділя випаде 1 вересня, то служба переноситься на попередню неділю, щоб не збігатися з іншими трьома службами, тобто недільною, Індикта і св. Симеона . Піст Усікновення не переносимо на неділю, а зберігаємо в самий день празника ."

The English says "of 24 June" but the Ukrainian says "24 липня" which is 24 July. That's a mistranslation. "липня" is July, not June. The English says "24 June", it should be "24 July". That's a semantic error. Also, the English says "All-Night Vigil" which is correct for "всенічним". The rest is accurate. So error: 24 липня → 24 July, not June.

Now the translation for 31 August:
English: "31 AUGUST Deposition of the Sash of the Most Holy Theotokos
Everything - according to the rule of the Deposition of the Robe 2. VII, here on p. 305-306."

Ukrainian: "31 СЕРПНЯ Покладення Пояса Пресвятої Богородиці
Все – за уставом Покладення Ризи 2.VІІ, тут на стор. 305-306."

This is accurate. "Sash" is a valid translation for Пояс (belt/sash). "Deposition of the Sash" is consistent with the feast title. "Deposition of the Robe" is correct for Ризи. "2.VII" is rendered as "2. VII" (that's fine). No errors.

Now, the bigger issue is that the English output contains a huge amount of text not requested, but we are not to flag that as an error if we are just auditing the translation of the given segment. The task is to compare the source segment with the translation segment. Since the translation segment includes many extra sections before the relevant dates, the relevant part that matches is only the 29 August and 31 August sections. But the initial English line "Everything - according to the general rule of a Saint with Polyeleos..." is part of the translation segment, but it is not in the source at all. That could be a dropped chunk from a previous date, but for this audit, we note that the translation segment does not correspond to the source segment; it appears to be a misaligned chunk. However, the instruction might be that the English translation segment provided is only the translation for the dates given? But the source starts with 29 August, so the translation should start with "29 AUGUST...". But the provided English translation begins with a different sentence, then 31 July, etc. This indicates that the English translation likely includes the preceding pages as well, not just the segment. But our task is to audit the given pair. We must note that the English translation segment contains material that is not a translation of the Ukrainian source segment. That is a critical mismatch. The system instructions require strict chunk boundary rules: "Stop Header Authority: The Next Chunk Title is the absolute hard stop." So if the translator was supposed to translate the chunk that starts with "29 СЕРПНЯ", they should not have included earlier content. This is a violation of the chunk boundary rule.

Now check for any dropped sentences in the specific 29 August lines: The source has "Переноситься звичайно на наступну неділю, тільки якщо наступна неділя випаде 1 вересня, то служба переноситься на попередню неділю, щоб не збігатися з іншими трьома службами, тобто недільною, Індикта і св. Симеона ." The English translates it fully. It includes "only if the following Sunday falls on 1 September, then the service is transferred to the previous Sunday". It then says "so as not to coincide with three other services, that is Resurrectional, of the Indiction and of St. Simeon". That is accurate. The Ukrainian mentions "трьома службами, тобто недільною, Індикта і св. Симеона". "недільною" means "Sunday service", so "Resurrectional" is appropriate. So no missing sentences.

Now check for prohibited terms. "All-Night Vigil" is canonical. "Forefeast", "Afterfeast", "Polyeleos", "Sessional hymn" used earlier in the irrelevant sections, but those are fine. "Theotokion" is canonical. No forbidden variants spotted. Capitalization: "Most Holy Theotokos" is capitalized, correct. Deity pronouns: In the translated parts that include divine address, they use correct capitalization (e.g., "Thy", "Thou"? Actually, the 29 Aug part doesn't have direct deity pronouns. So okay.

The mistake with "24 June" vs "24 July" is a clear error. Also possibly the translation of "липня" as June is a factual error.

Now, regarding the 31 July section that appears in the translation but not in source: that is an extraneous addition. Should we flag it as an error? The instruction says: "Identify: 1. Missing sentences or dropped concepts. 2. Semantic inaccuracies or mistranslations. 3. Violations of liturgical terminology rules... 4. Pronoun and deity capitalization rule violations." So we should report that the English segment includes a large block of text that is not present in the source segment, which is a violation of the 1:1 output rule. That could be considered a chunk boundary error, but technically the source segment didn't include that content, and the translation added it. So it's extraneous. However, the task is to compare the source to the translation; if the translation contains extra material not in source, we can note it as a mismatch. But the problematic line "Everything - according to the general rule of a Saint with Polyeleos..." is completely out of place. That might be from a previous date (maybe 24 June or something). So it's a dropped or inserted content.

We'll list the issues:

- The English translation begins with text not present in the source segment, breaking chunk boundary rule and not matching the source. Specifically, the line "Everything - according to the general rule of a Saint with Polyeleos..." through the entire section up to "29 AUGUST" is not a translation of any part of the provided Ukrainian source. This constitutes a violation of the strict 1:1 output rule.
- For the 29 August entry: the phrase "according to the rule of 24 June" is a mistranslation. The Ukrainian reads "24 липня" (24 July). The correct translation is "24 July". This is a semantic inaccuracy. (If the typikon indeed refers to a rule for June, the source says July, so must be July.)
- All liturgical terms in the 29 August and 31 August entries are compliant. No forbidden variants detected.
- Capitalization and pronoun rules appear satisfied (no violations in the relevant parts).

So the audit findings will mention the chunk boundary violation and the July->June mistranslation.

Now, we need to output as a concise markdown list. So:

- **Extraneous content / Chunk boundary violation**: The English translation segment begins with a sentence and entire sections (31 July, 1 August, 6 August, 15 August, 16 August) that do not appear in the Ukrainian source segment. This violates the strict 1:1 output rule and indicates the translation is not aligned with the source chunk.
- **Mistranslation of "24 липня"**: In the 29 August translation, "24 June" is incorrect; it should be "24 July".
- No other semantic inaccuracies, missing sentences, or terminology violations in the portions that do correspond to the source.

We'll output that.

### Audit Findings
- **Extraneous Content / Chunk Boundary Violation:** The English translation segment opens with a sentence (*“Everything – according to the general rule of a Saint with Polyeleos…”*) and an entire block covering 31 July, 1 August, 6 August, 15 August, and 16 August. None of this material is present in the Ukrainian source segment provided. This violates the strict 1:1 translation rule and indicates a misalignment between the source chunk and the translated output.

- **Mistranslation of “24 липня” (29 August entry):** The Ukrainian text specifies *“Все – за уставом 24 липня”*. The English translation renders this as *“Everything – according to the rule of 24 June”*. “липня” means **July**, not June. The correct phrase should be **“24 July”**.

- No missing sentences, liturgical‑term violations, or capitalization/pronoun errors were found in the portions of the translation that actually correspond to the source (29 August and 31 August).
